##### FILE: Clutch-Identity-MYSQL-Deployment.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/clutch-idty-mysql-deployment:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: clutch-idty-mysql-deployment
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: mysql
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: mysql
    spec:
      containers:
      - env:
        - name: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: password
              name: clutch-idty-mysql-secret
        image: mysql:latest
        name: mysql
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3306
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-persistent-storage
      volumes:
      - name: mysql-persistent-storage
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: clutch-idty-mysql-pvc

---

##### FILE: Clutch-Ingress.yaml #####

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Ingress/clutch-idty-ingress:
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  annotations:
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/rewrite-target: /
  name: clutch-idty-ingress
  namespace: default
spec:
  rules:
  - host: clutch.com
    http:
      paths:
      - backend:
          service:
            name: clutch-identity-clusterip-srv
            port:
              number: 80
        path: /api/identity
        pathType: Prefix
      - backend:
          service:
            name: clutch-employee-clusterip-srv
            port:
              number: 80
        path: /api/employee
        pathType: Prefix
      - backend:
          service:
            name: clutch-position-clusterip-srv
            port:
              number: 80
        path: /api/position
        pathType: Prefix

##### FILE: cm.aggregate-responses.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/ConfigMap/aggregate-responses:
apiVersion: v1
data:
  script.js: "var year = parseInt(process.env[\"YEAR\"]);\nvar month = parseInt(process.env[\"MONTH\"]);\n\nvar
    dateFrom = new Date(year + \"-\" + month + \"-1Z\");\nvar dateTo = new Date(dateFrom);\ndateTo.setMonth(dateTo.getMonth()
    + 1);\n\nprint(\"Processing quiz responses - in month \" + month);\nprint(\"==============================================\");\nprint();\nprint(\"Year:
    \ \" + year);\nprint(\"Month: \" + month);\nprint();\nprint(\"Query range:\");\nprint(\"
    \ From: \" + dateFrom);\nprint(\"  To:   \" + dateTo);\nprint();\nprint(\"Results:\")\n\nvar
    cursor = db.responses.aggregate(\n  {\n    $match: {\n      timestamp: { $gte:
    dateFrom, $lt: dateTo }\n    }\n  },\n  {\n    $group: {\n      _id: { $dateTrunc:
    { date: \"$timestamp\", unit: \"day\" } },\n      totalCount: { $sum: 1 },\n      correctCount:
    { $sum: { $cond: { if: \"$correct\", then: 1, else: 0 } } },\n      incorrectCount:
    { $sum: { $cond: { if: \"$correct\", then: 0, else: 1 } } },\n    }\n  }\n);\n\nvar
    matched = 0;\nvar inserted = 0;\nvar updated = 0;\nif (cursor.hasNext()) {\n  while
    (cursor.hasNext()) {\n    var result = cursor.next();\n    print(\"  \" + JSON.stringify(result));\n\n
    \   var writeResult = db.statistics.replaceOne(\n        {_id: result._id},\n
    \       result,\n        { upsert: true }\n    );\n    matched += writeResult.matchedCount;\n
    \   inserted += writeResult.upsertedCount;\n    updated += writeResult.modifiedCount;\n
    \ }\n  cursor.close();\n\n  print();\n  print(\"Matched: \" + matched + \"; Updated:
    \" + updated + \"; Inserted: \" + inserted); \n} else {\n  print(\"  No responses
    found.\");\n}\n\nvar sleepSeconds = Math.floor(30 + Math.random() * 30); \nprint();\nprint(\"Waiting
    \" + sleepSeconds + \"s to simulate long-running task.\");\nsleep(sleepSeconds
    * 1000);\n\nprint();\nprint(\"Done.\");\n"
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  labels:
    app: aggregate-responses
  name: aggregate-responses
  namespace: default

---

##### FILE: cm41.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/ConfigMap/mongodb-configmap:
apiVersion: v1
data:
  ensure-users.js: |
    const targetDbStr = 'test';
    const rootUser = cat('/etc/k8-test/admin/MONGO_ROOT_USERNAME');
    const rootPass = cat('/etc/k8-test/admin/MONGO_ROOT_PASSWORD');
    const usersStr = cat('/etc/k8-test/MONGO_USERS_LIST');
    const adminDb = db.getSiblingDB('admin');
    adminDb.auth(rootUser, rootPass);
    print('Successfully authenticated admin user');
    const targetDb = db.getSiblingDB(targetDbStr);
    const customRoles = adminDb
      .getRoles({rolesInfo: 1, showBuiltinRoles: false})
      .map(role => role.role)
      .filter(Boolean);
    usersStr
      .trim()
      .split(';')
      .map(s => s.split(':'))
      .forEach(user => {
        const username = user[0];
        const rolesStr = user[1];
        const password = user[2];
        if (!rolesStr || !password) {
          return;
        }
        const roles = rolesStr.split(',');
        const userDoc = {
          user: username,
          pwd: password,
        };
        userDoc.roles = roles.map(role => {
          if (!~customRoles.indexOf(role)) {
            return role;
          }
          return {role: role, db: 'admin'};
        });
        try {
          targetDb.createUser(userDoc);
        } catch (err) {
          if (!~err.message.toLowerCase().indexOf('duplicate')) {
            throw err;
          }
        }
      });
  mongo.conf: |
    storage:
      dbPath: /data/db
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: mongodb-configmap
  namespace: default

---


Mutation:
Mutation has been applied successfully.
pass: 0, fail: 0, warn: 0, error: 0, skip: 0

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/deployment-test:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app: front
  name: deployment-test
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: front
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: front
    spec:
      containers:
      - env:
        - name: DB_HOST
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: db_host
              name: vars
        - name: DB_USER
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: db_user
              name: vars
        image: nginx:alpine
        name: nginx
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /etc/nginx/conf.d
          name: nginx-vol
        - mountPath: /opt
          name: script-vol
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          items:
          - key: nginx
            path: default.conf
          name: nginx-config
        name: nginx-vol
      - configMap:
          items:
          - key: script
            path: script.sh
          name: vars
        name: script-vol

---

##### FILE: cm-sample.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/ConfigMap/sample-cm:
apiVersion: v1
data:
  sample.js: |
    import { browser } from 'k6/experimental/browser';
    import { check } from 'k6';

    export const options = {
        scenarios: {
            ui: {
                executor: 'constant-vus',
                options: {
                    browser: {
                        type: 'chromium'
                    }
                },
                vus: 1,
                duration: '30s'
            }
        }
    };


    export default async function () {
        const page = browser.newPage();
        try {
            await page.goto('https://test.legalmatch.com/');
            page.screenshot({ path: 'screenshot.png' });
            check(page, {
                'Find the Right Lawyer for Your Legal Issue!': (page) =>
                    page.locator("(//a[@class='case-intake-form__header--link'])[1]").isVisible() ===
                    true
            });

            check(page, {
                'Hero Banner': (page) => page.locator("(//div[@class='hero '])[1]").isVisible() === true
            });

            check(page, {
                'Top Rated': (page) =>
                    page
                        .locator("(//div[@class='w-top-rated w-top-rated--no-location '])[1]")
                        .isVisible() === true
            });
            page.waitForTimeout(5000);
        } finally {
            page.close();
        }
    }
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: sample-cm
  namespace: default

---


Mutation:
Mutation has been applied successfully.
pass: 0, fail: 0, warn: 0, error: 0, skip: 0

##### FILE: cockroachdb-statefulset_3.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/StatefulSet/cockroachdb:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  labels:
    app: cockroachdb
  name: cockroachdb
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: cockroachdb
  serviceName: cockroachdb
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: cockroachdb
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: app
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - cockroachdb
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 100
      containers:
      - command:
        - /bin/bash
        - -ecx
        - |
          # The use of qualified `hostname -f` is crucial:
          # Other nodes aren't able to look up the unqualified hostname.
          CRARGS=("start" "--logtostderr" "--insecure" "--host" "$(hostname -f)" "--http-host" "0.0.0.0")
          # We only want to initialize a new cluster (by omitting the join flag)
          # if we're sure that we're the first node (i.e. index 0) and that
          # there aren't any other nodes running as part of the cluster that
          # this is supposed to be a part of (which indicates that a cluster
          # already exists and we should make sure not to create a new one).
          # It's fine to run without --join on a restart if there aren't any
          # other nodes.
          if [ ! "$(hostname)" == "cockroachdb-0" ] || \
             [ -e "/cockroach/cockroach-data/cluster_exists_marker" ]
          then
            # We don't join cockroachdb in order to avoid a node attempting
            # to join itself, which currently doesn't work
            # (https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/issues/9625).
            CRARGS+=("--join" "cockroachdb-public")
          fi
          exec /cockroach/cockroach ${CRARGS[*]}
        image: cockroachdb/cockroach:v1.1.0
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: cockroachdb
        ports:
        - containerPort: 26257
          name: grpc
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /cockroach/cockroach-data
          name: datadir
      initContainers:
      - args:
        - -on-start=/on-start.sh
        - -service=cockroachdb
        env:
        - name: POD_NAMESPACE
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.namespace
        image: cockroachdb/cockroach-k8s-init:0.2
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: bootstrap
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /cockroach/cockroach-data
          name: datadir
      terminationGracePeriodSeconds: 60
      volumes:
      - name: datadir
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: datadir
  volumeClaimTemplates:
  - metadata:
      name: datadir
    spec:
      accessModes:
      - ReadWriteOnce
      resources:
        requests:
          storage: 1Gi

---

##### FILE: cockroachdb-statefulset2_9.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/StatefulSet/cockroachdb:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  name: cockroachdb
  namespace: default
spec:
  podManagementPolicy: Parallel
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: cockroachdb
  serviceName: cockroachdb
  template:
    metadata:
      annotations:
        cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/safe-to-evict: "true"
      labels:
        app: cockroachdb
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: app
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - cockroachdb
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 100
      containers:
      - command:
        - /bin/bash
        - -ecx
        - exec /cockroach/cockroach start --logtostderr --certs-dir /cockroach/cockroach-certs
          --advertise-host $(hostname -f) --http-addr 0.0.0.0 --join cockroachdb-0.cockroachdb,cockroachdb-1.cockroachdb,cockroachdb-2.cockroachdb
          $(cat /etc/cockroach-locality/locality || true) --cache $(expr $MEMORY_LIMIT_MIB
          / 4)MiB --max-sql-memory $(expr $MEMORY_LIMIT_MIB / 4)MiB
        env:
        - name: COCKROACH_CHANNEL
          value: kubernetes-secure
        - name: GOMAXPROCS
          valueFrom:
            resourceFieldRef:
              divisor: "1"
              resource: limits.cpu
        - name: MEMORY_LIMIT_MIB
          valueFrom:
            resourceFieldRef:
              divisor: 1Mi
              resource: limits.memory
        image: cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.0
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: cockroachdb
        ports:
        - containerPort: 26257
          name: grpc
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
        readinessProbe:
          failureThreshold: 2
          httpGet:
            path: /health?ready=1
            port: http
            scheme: HTTPS
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
          periodSeconds: 5
        resources:
          limits:
            cpu: "5"
            memory: 20Gi
          requests:
            cpu: "5"
            memory: 20Gi
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /cockroach/cockroach-data
          name: datadir
        - mountPath: /cockroach/cockroach-certs
          name: certs
        - mountPath: /etc/cockroach-locality
          name: cockroach-locality
          readOnly: true
      initContainers:
      - env:
        - name: KUBERNETES_NODE
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: spec.nodeName
        image: cockroachdb/locality-checker:0.1
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: locality-checker
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /etc/cockroach-locality
          name: cockroach-locality
      serviceAccountName: cockroachdb
      terminationGracePeriodSeconds: 60

##### FILE: cockroachdb-statefulset3_6.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/StatefulSet/cockroachdb:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  name: cockroachdb
  namespace: default
spec:
  podManagementPolicy: Parallel
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: cockroachdb
  serviceName: cockroachdb
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: cockroachdb
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: app
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - cockroachdb
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 100
      containers:
      - command:
        - /bin/bash
        - -ecx
        - exec /cockroach/cockroach start --logtostderr --certs-dir /cockroach/cockroach-certs
          --advertise-host $(hostname -f) --http-addr 0.0.0.0 --join cockroachdb-0.cockroachdb,cockroachdb-1.cockroachdb,cockroachdb-2.cockroachdb
          --cache $(expr $MEMORY_LIMIT_MIB / 4)MiB --max-sql-memory $(expr $MEMORY_LIMIT_MIB
          / 4)MiB
        env:
        - name: COCKROACH_CHANNEL
          value: kubernetes-secure
        - name: GOMAXPROCS
          valueFrom:
            resourceFieldRef:
              divisor: "1"
              resource: limits.cpu
        - name: MEMORY_LIMIT_MIB
          valueFrom:
            resourceFieldRef:
              divisor: 1Mi
              resource: limits.memory
        image: cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.4
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: cockroachdb
        ports:
        - containerPort: 26257
          name: grpc
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
        readinessProbe:
          failureThreshold: 2
          httpGet:
            path: /health?ready=1
            port: http
            scheme: HTTPS
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
          periodSeconds: 5
        resources:
          limits:
            cpu: "2"
            memory: 8Gi
          requests:
            cpu: "2"
            memory: 8Gi
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /cockroach/cockroach-data
          name: datadir
        - mountPath: /cockroach/cockroach-certs
          name: certs
      serviceAccountName: cockroachdb
      terminationGracePeriodSeconds: 60
      volumes:
      - name: datadir
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: datadir
      - name: certs
        secret:
          defaultMode: 256
          secretName: cockroachdb.node
  updateStrategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
  volumeClaimTemplates:
  - metadata:
      name: datadir
    spec:
      accessModes:
      - ReadWriteOnce
      resources:
        requests:
          storage: 100Gi

##### FILE: cockroachdb-statefulset4_3.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/StatefulSet/cockroachdb:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  labels:
    app: cockroachdb
  name: cockroachdb
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: cockroachdb
  serviceName: cockroachdb
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: cockroachdb
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: app
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - cockroachdb
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 100
      containers:
      - command:
        - /bin/bash
        - -ecx
        - |
          # The use of qualified `hostname -f` is crucial:
          # Other nodes aren't able to look up the unqualified hostname.
          CRARGS=("start" "--logtostderr" "--insecure" "--host" "$(hostname -f)" "--http-host" "0.0.0.0")
          # We only want to initialize a new cluster (by omitting the join flag)
          # if we're sure that we're the first node (i.e. index 0) and that
          # there aren't any other nodes running as part of the cluster that
          # this is supposed to be a part of (which indicates that a cluster
          # already exists and we should make sure not to create a new one).
          # It's fine to run without --join on a restart if there aren't any
          # other nodes.
          if [ ! "$(hostname)" == "cockroachdb-0" ] || \
             [ -e "/cockroach/cockroach-data/cluster_exists_marker" ]
          then
            # We don't join cockroachdb in order to avoid a node attempting
            # to join itself, which currently doesn't work
            # (https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/issues/9625).
            CRARGS+=("--join" "cockroachdb-public")
          fi
          exec /cockroach/cockroach ${CRARGS[*]}
        image: cockroachdb/cockroach:v1.1.0
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: cockroachdb
        ports:
        - containerPort: 26257
          name: grpc
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /cockroach/cockroach-data
          name: datadir
      initContainers:
      - args:
        - -on-start=/on-start.sh
        - -service=cockroachdb
        env:
        - name: POD_NAMESPACE
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.namespace
        image: cockroachdb/cockroach-k8s-init:0.2
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: bootstrap
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /cockroach/cockroach-data
          name: datadir
      terminationGracePeriodSeconds: 60
      volumes:
      - name: datadir
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: datadir
  volumeClaimTemplates:
  - metadata:
      name: datadir
    spec:
      accessModes:
      - ReadWriteOnce
      resources:
        requests:
          storage: 1Gi

---
